Jamison Brereton

51 (877)
Dialogue between Agni and the Gods
Agni Sauc─лka
9 verses: triс╣гс╣нubh
The classic dialogue between Agni and the gods (or one or more gods: he addresses Mitra and Varuс╣Зa [vs. 2] and Varuс╣Зa alone [vss. 4, 6]). Agni appears still to be in the waters (or just emerged), and the gods have only recently discovered his hiding place. The first question is which god spotted him (vss. 1тАУ3). Agni then describes the fear that drove him from his sacrificial role, in responsive language that defines an omphalos (vss. 4, 6, esp. 4a and 6c). In the omphalos verse (5) the gods make the argument that Manu, a human and the first sacrificer, deserves to have his sacrifice completed by AgniтАЩs conveyance of the oblations. It is striking that the gods, perhaps disingenuously, do not argue for their own deserving state. In the last three verses (7тАУ9) the gods propose rewards for AgniтАЩs returning to his task, and he accepts them.

рдорд╛рдирд╕рддрд░рдЩреНрдЧрд┐рдгреАрдХреГрддреН - рдЯрд┐рдкреНрдкрдиреА

The mention of the archer shooting at the bull is important. It is an ancient motif in myth that is depicted in Egypt on the Dendera Zodiac. Here the goddess Satit shoots at Sirius which is the head of the Sothis cow! But in this instance the gaur bull is likely to be Taurus fleeing from the archer who is mR^igavyAdha (or could he gaur be another name for the antelope mR^iga?) for the Indo-Aryans.

English translation:

тАЬ(The gods speak). Great and very dense is the covering enveloped by which, Agni, you have enteredinto the waters. Agni J─Бtavedas, one deity has beheld all your manifold forms.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Taittir─лya Saс╣Гhit─Б 2.6.6: Agnihad three elder brothers, who were killed by the Vaс╣гaс╣нk─Бra (utterance of vaс╣гaс╣н!) in the form of a thunderbolt,and by Havirv─Бhana (conveyance of oblations to the gods), the oblation bearer of the gods. Agni ┼Ъaucika,afraid of sharing the fate of his elder brothers, fled and his himself in the deep water. рд╕рд╛рдпрдг-рднрд╛рд╖реНрдпрдореН

рдЗрджрдордЧреНрдиреЗрд░реНрд╡рд╛рдХреНрдпрдореН ред рдПрдХреЛ рджреЗрд╡реЛрд╜рдкрд╢реНрдпрджрд┐рддреНрдпреБрдХреНрддреЗ рдкреГрдЪреНрдЫрддрд┐ ред рдХреЛ рдорд╛ рдорд╛рдВ рджрджрд░реНрд╢ рджреГрд╖реНрдЯрд╡рд╛рдиреН ред рд╕ рджреЗрд╡рдГ рдХрддрдордГ рдпреЛ рдореЗ рдордо рддрдиреНрд╡рдГ рддрдиреВрдГ рдмрд╣реБрдзрд╛ рдмрд╣реБрдкреНрд░рдХрд╛рд░рдВ рд╕реНрдерд┐рддрд╛рдГ рдкрд░реНрдпрдкрд╢реНрдпрддреН рдкрд░рд┐рджреГрд╖реНрдЯрд╡рд╛рдиреН ред рд╣реЗ рдорд┐рддреНрд░рд╛рд╡рд░реБрдгрд╛ рдорд┐рддреНрд░рд╛рд╡рд░реБрдгреМ рдЕрдЧреНрдиреЗрдГ рдордо рд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд╡рд╛рдГ рд╕рд░реНрд╡рд╛рдГ рд╕рдорд┐рдзрдГ рджреАрдкреНрддрд╛рдГ рджреЗрд╡рдпрд╛рдиреАрдГ рджреЗрд╡рдпрд╛рдирд╕рд╛рдзрдирднреВрддрд╛рдГ рддрдиреНрд╡реЛ рджреГрд╖реНрдЯрд╛ рдЗрддреНрдпреБрдХреНрддрдВ рдпрджрд┐ рджреГрд╖реНрдЯрд╛рд╢реНрдЪреЗрддреНрддрд░реНрд╣рд┐ рдХреНрд╡ рдХреНрд╖рд┐рдпрдиреНрддрд┐ рдХреНрд╡ рдирд┐рд╡рд╕рдиреНрддреАрддреНрдпреЗрд╡рдВ рджреЗрд╡рд╛рдирд╛рдВ рдкреБрд░рддреЛ рд╡рд░реНрддрдорд╛рдиреМ рдорд┐рддреНрд░рд╛рд╡рд░реБрдгрд╛рд╡рд╛рд╣рд╛рдЧреНрдирд┐рдГ рее

рдорд╛рдирд╕рддрд░рдЩреНрдЧрд┐рдгреАрдХреГрддреН

[agni asks the devas:] Which God had seen me? Who of all their multitude saw my forms in many dwellings? Where then are placed the fire sticks of agni that lead one of the northern path of the ecliptic (devayAna) O varuNa and mitra?

рдорд╛рдирд╕рддрд░рдЩреНрдЧрд┐рдгреАрдХреГрддреН - рдЯрд┐рдкреНрдкрдиреА

These cryptically allude exactly to what de Santillana and von Dechend mention as the armillary sphere of the sky with agni as the equinotical colure. The point where he enters the waters is the intersection with the celestial equator. They mention that the Aztecs took Castor and Pollux to be the fire sticks from which men learned to make fire.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬ(Agni speaks). Who has beheld me? Which is it of the deities who has fully seen my manifold forms?Where Mitra and Varuс╣Зa, do Agni’s luminous vehicles of the gods abide?тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

[Agni:] Who saw me? Which one was that god who fully saw my bodies in their multiple forms?
Where indeed, o Mitra and Varuс╣Зa, are all the kindling sticks of Agni lying, which lead to the gods?

Griffith

What God hath seen me? Who of all their number clearly beheld my forms in many places?
Where lie, then, all the sacred logs of Agni that lead him God-ward, Varuna and Mitra?

Geldner

Wer hat mich gesehen, welcher ist es unter den G├╢ttern, der meine Leiber vielfach erschaut hat? Mitra und Varuna! Wo bleiben doch all die Brennh├╢lzer des Agni, auf denen er seinen Weg zu den G├╢ttern geht?

Grassmann

┬╗Wer von den G├╢ttern war’s, der mich erblickt hat, der meine Glieder hier und dort gesehn hat? Wo weilen jetzt die Feuerflammen alle, die G├╢ttern nahten, Varuna und Mitra?┬л

рдорд╛рдирд╕рддрд░рдЩреНрдЧрд┐рдгреАрдХреГрддреН

[varUNa on behalf of the devas said:] In many places, we searched for you O agni jAtavedas, hidden in the plants and waters. Then yama piled you*, one with many-colored [flames], blazing forth from your tenfold secret station,
*(achikech: the same root as chayana as in agni-chayana the piling of fire altar)

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬ(The gods). We sought for you, Agni J─Бtavedas, who had entered in many ways into the waters, intothe plural nts; Yama recognized you, who have adorable rays, blazing from your ten hiding-plural ces.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

These are thethree worlds– heaven, mid-air, earth; three divinities, Agni, V─Бyu, ─Аditya; the waters, the shrubs, the trees, andthe bodies of living beings

Jamison Brereton

[Gods:] We sought you in multiple places, o J─Бtavedas, you who had entered into the waters, into the plants, o Agni.
Yama espied you, o bright-beamed one, shining out farther than (a
distance) of ten stages.

Griffith

Then Yama marked thee, God of wondrous splendour! effulgent from thy tenfold secret dwelling,

рд╕рд╛рдпрдг-рднрд╛рд╖реНрдпрдореН

рдЕрдирдпрд╛ рджреЗрд╡рд╛ рдорд╛рдВ рдЬреНрдЮрд╛рддрд╡рдиреНрдд рдЗрддрд┐ рдирд┐рд╢реНрдЪрд┐рддреНрдп рдЧреВрд╣рдирд╕реНрдп рдкреНрд░рдпреЛрдЬрдирдорд╛рд╣ ред рд╣реЗ рд╡рд░реБрдг рджреЗрд╡ рдЕрд╣рдВ рд╣реЛрддреНрд░рд╛рддреН рд╣реЛрддрд╡реНрдпрд╛рддреН ред рд╣рд╡рд┐рд░реНрд╡рд╣рдирд╛рджрд┐рддреНрдпрд░реНрдердГ ред рддрд╕реНрдорд╛рддреН рдмрд┐рднреНрдпрддреН рдЖрдпрдореН рдЖрдЧрддрд╡рд╛рдирд╕реНрдорд┐ ред рдЕрддрдГ рдорд╛ рдорд╛рдореН рдПрд╡ рдПрд╡рдВ рдкреВрд░реНрд╡рдкреНрд░рдХрд╛рд░реЗрдг рдЕрддреНрд░ рдЕрд╕реНрдорд┐рдиреН рд╣рд╡рд┐рд░реНрд╡рд╣рдиреЗ рдиреЗрддреН рдпреБрдирдЬрдиреН рдиреИрд╡ рдпреЛрдЬрдпрдиреНрддреБ рджреЗрд╡рд╛рдГ ред рддрд╕реНрдп рддрд╛рджреГрд╢рд╕реНрдп рдмрд┐рднреНрдпрддрдГ рдореЗ рддрдиреНрд╡реЛ рдмрд╣реБрдзрд╛ рдирд┐рд╡рд┐рд╖реНрдЯрд╛рдГ рдЕрдкреНрд╕реБ ред рдПрддрдорд░реНрдердореН рдПрддрджреНрдзрд╡рд┐рд░реНрд╡рд╣рдирдХрд╛рд░реНрдпрдореН рдЕрдЧреНрдирд┐рдГ рдЕрд╣рдВ рди рдЪрд┐рдХреЗрдд рди рдмреБрдзреНрдпреЗ рдирд╛рдЩреНрдЧреАрдХрд░реЛрдорд┐ рее

рдорд╛рдирд╕рддрд░рдЩреНрдЧрд┐рдгреАрдХреГрддреН

[agni said:] O varuNa, I fled in fear from the sacrifice,so that gods do not in this manner yoke me*. Thus my forms we laid down in many places; I, agni saw this as my path.
* yoke me= enjoin to the sacrificial rite

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬ(Agni). Divine Varuс╣Зa, I have come hither, being afraid of hot─Б, lest the gods should again associateme with him; my forms have therefore entered (into the waters) in various plural ces. I, Agni, do not consent (toundertake) that office.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Hotr─Б: i.e., havirv─Бhana, who seems here to be a person n

Jamison Brereton

[Agni:] I went in fear of the Hotarship, Varuс╣Зa, lest the gods yoke me to it.
My bodies settled down in multiple places. I, Agni, do not attend to this business.

Griffith

I fled in fear from sacrificial worship, Varuna, lest the Gods should thus engage me.
Thus were my forms laid down in many places. This, as my goal, I Agni saw before me.

Geldner

Aus Furcht vor dem Hotri-Amt bin ich gegangen, Varuna, damit mich nicht die G├╢tter daran einspannen k├╢nnen. So sind meine Leiber vielfach ins Wasser eingegangen. Ich, Agni, denke nicht mehr an dieses Gesch├дft.

Grassmann

┬╗Ich floh vom Opfer, Varuna, bef├╝rchtend, dass wieder mich die G├╢tter daran b├дnden, Drum barg ich hier und dorthin meine Glieder, ich Agni, hab’ nicht mehr solch Werk im Sinne.┬л

рдмреНрд░рд╣реНрдордореБрдирд┐ - рдкрджрд╛рд░реНрдердГ

рдорд╛рдирд╕рддрд░рдЩреНрдЧрд┐рдгреАрдХреГрддреН

[varUNa on behalf of the devas said:] Come OтАЩ agni who dwells in the darkness; manu devoted to the gods desiring to perform sacrifices,waits ready to do rituals. Make clear the paths leading to the northern course of the ecliptic, and bear oblations with good-will.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬ(The gods). Come, Agni, the devout Manu (is) desirous of offering sacrifice; adorning yourself, youabide in darkness; make straight the paths traversed by the gods, and with a benevolent mind convey ouroblations.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

[Gods:] Come here! Manu, devoted to the gods, has desire for sacrifice, having properly prepared it. Yet you dwell in darkness, Agni.
Make the paths leading to the gods easily passable. Convey the oblations, showing your benevolence.

Griffith

Come; man is pious and would fain do worship, he waits prepared: in gloom thou, Agni, dwellest.
Make pathways leading God-ward clear and easy, and bear oblations with a kindly spirit.

Geldner

Komm her, der gottergebene Manu w├╝nscht zu opfern und hat alles in Bereitschaft. Du weilst noch im Dunklen. Mach die Wege, die zu den G├╢ttern gehen, gangbar; ├╝berbringe geneigten Sinnes die Opfer!

Grassmann

Komm her, der fromme Mensch das Opfer liebend steht schon bereit; was weilst du in dem Dunkel? Mach gangbar nun die gottbetretnen Wege, und fahre wohlgemuth die Opfertr├дnke.

Elizarenkova

рдорд╛рдирд╕рддрд░рдЩреНрдЧрд┐рдгреАрдХреГрддреН

[agni said:] My elder brothers first selected this path, a circuit, like the circumambulation of a charioteer. So,varuNa, I fled afar in fear, as the wild bull (Gaur) flees from the archerтАЩs bowstring. (The elder brothers of agni are the previous equinoctial points that slipped away from precession and thus тАЬdiedтАЭ)

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬ(Agni). The elder brothers of Agni performed that duty, as the driver of a chariot covers the roaс╕Н(They were slain), and therefore, Varuс╣Зa, I fled afar through fear. I trembled as a wild ox (tembles) at thebowstring of the archer.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Elder brothers of Agni: were named Bh┼лpati, Bhuvanapati and Bh┼лt─Бn─Бmpati

Jamison Brereton

[Agni:] The brothers of Agni earlier kept rolling along after this business, like a charioteer along the road.
In fear of this, Varuс╣Зa, I went far away. I flinched from it like a buffalo from the bowstring of an archer.

Griffith

This goal mine elder brothers erst selected, as he who drives a car the way to travel.
So,Varuna, I fled afar through terror, as flies the wild-bull from an archer’s bowstring.

рдЗрджрдВ рджреЗрд╡рд╛рдирд╛рдВ рд╡рд╛рдХреНрдпрдореН ред рд╣реЗ рдЕрдЧреНрдиреЗ рдпрддреН рдЖрдпреБрдГ рдЖрдпреБрд╖реНрдпрдореН рдЕрдЬрд░рдВ рдЬрд░рд╛рд░рд╣рд┐рддрдорд╕реНрддрд┐ рддрддреН рддреЗ рдХреБрд░реНрдордГ ред рдпреБрдХреНрддрдГ рддреЗрдирд╛рдпреБрд╖рд╛ рд╕рдВрдпреБрдХреНрддрд╕реНрддреНрд╡рдВ рд╣реЗ рдЬрд╛рддрд╡реЗрджрдГ рдЬрд╛рддрдкреНрд░рдЬреНрдЮ рдпрдерд╛ рди рд░рд┐рд╖реНрдпрд╛рдГ рди рдореНрд░рд┐рдпрд╕реЗ рддрдерд╛ рдХреБрд░реНрдордГред рдЕрде рд╡рд╣рд╛рд╕рд┐ рд╡рд╣ рд╕реБрдордирд╕реНрдпрдорд╛рдирдГ рд╕реМрдордирд╕реНрдпрдВ рдХреБрд░реНрд╡рдиреН рд╡реЛрдврд╡реНрдпрдВ рд╡рд╣рдиреН ред рддрджреЗрд╡ рджрд░реНрд╢рдпрддрд┐ ред рд╣рд╡рд┐рд╖рдГ рдпрдЬрдорд╛рдирдкреНрд░рддреНрддрд╕реНрдп рднрд╛рдЧрдореН ред рдХреЗрднреНрдпрдГ ред рджреЗрд╡реЗрднреНрдпрдГ ред рд╣реЗ рд╕реБрдЬрд╛рдд рд╢реЛрднрдирдЬрдиреНрдордиреНрдирдЧреНрдиреЗ рее

рдорд╛рдирд╕рддрд░рдЩреНрдЧрд┐рдгреАрдХреГрддреН

[varUNa on behalf of the devas said:] O agni jAtadvedas we establish for you undecaying life, so that when you are thus employed you are not harmed. So, well-born one you shall with good-will bear to the gods their share of oblations.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬ(The gods). We grant you life, Agni, which (is) exempt from decay, so that thus endowed, J─Бtavedas,you will not die; so, becoming conciliated, well- born, Agni, bear their portion of the oblation to the gods.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

[Gods:] We will make a lifetime for you, which is free from old age, Agni, so that yoked (to your task) you will not suffer harm, J─Бtavedas.
Then will you, showing your benevolence, convey their portion of the oblation to the gods, o well-born one?

Griffith

We give thee life unwasting, Jatavedas, so that, employed, thou never shalt be injured.
So, nobly born! shalt thou with kindly spirit bear to the Gods their share of men’s oblations.

Geldner

Wir bereiten dir ein Leben, das alterlos ist, Agni, auf da├Я du eingespannt nicht zu Schaden kommest, o Jatavedas. Und du sollst geneigten Sinnes den G├╢ttern ihren Anteil am Opfer ├╝berbringen, du Wohlgeborener!

Grassmann

Wir schaffen dir, o Agni, ew’ge Jugend, dass, Wesenkenner, du im Dienst nicht leidest, Drum fahre nun auch wohlgemuth, o edler, hin zu den G├╢ttern ihren Opferantheil.

Elizarenkova

рдорд╛рдирд╕рддрд░рдЩреНрдЧрд┐рдгреАрдХреГрддреН

[agni said:] Grant me the fore-offerings and post-offerings*, and the sole-offerings and the shares of the strengthening oblations. [grant me] ghee, the waters, men and plants, and let me agni have long life, O gods, to Agni.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬ(Agni). Only grant to me, deities, the concentrated portion of the oblation the Pray─Бjas and Anuy─Бjasexclusively; (give me) the butter (the essence) of the waters, and man (the essence) of the plural nts; and let the lifeof Agni be long.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

The Pray─Бjas and the Anuy─Бjas: Pray─Бjas are the portion of the oblation which are to beoffered before the pradh─Бna (?principal ceremony), anuy─Бjas after it. urjasvantam haviс╣гo bh─Бgam, the strongportion of the haviс╣г, is that called sviс╣гс╣нakс╣Ыt, the concentrated portion of all the ingredients, the caru purod─Б┼Ыaetc., after the sprinkling afresh (pratyabhigh─Бraс╣Зa)

Jamison Brereton

[Agni:] Give the fore-offerings and the after-offerings exclusively to me, the nourishing portion of the oblation,
and the тАЬgheeтАЭ of the waters and the тАЬmanтАЭ of the plants, and let there be a long lifetime for Agni, o gods.

Griffith

Grant me the first oblations and the latter, entire, my forceful shares of holy presents,
The soul of plants, the fatness of the waters, and let there be long life, ye Gods, to Agni.

Geldner

Gebt mir die Voropfer und die Nachopfer ausschlie├Яlich zu eigen, den nahrhaften Teil des Opfers, und das Schmalz der Wasser und den Mann der Pflanzen, und langes Leben soll dem Agni werden, ihr G├╢tter!

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬ(The gods). Yours, Agni, be the Pray─Бjas and Anuy─Бjas exclusively; yours be the concentrated portions of the oblations; let this sacrifice; Agni, be all yours, and let the four quarters of space bow down beforeyou.тАЭ

рдорд╛рдирд╕рддрд░рдЩреНрдЧрд┐рдгреАрдХреГрддреН

[varUNa on behalf of the devas said:][agni said:] Yours are the fore-offerings and post-offerings*, and the sole-offerings and the shares of the strengthening oblations. O agni let this whole sacrificial rite belong to you, and let the four directions bow before thee.

*The fore- and after-offerings are the pra-yAjas and anu-yAja oblations made in the aprI rite. The kevala is the agni-only offering in the main course of the ritual.

Jamison Brereton

[Gods:] Yours be the fore-offerings and the after-offerings exclusively, the nourishing portions of the oblation;
yours, Agni, be this whole sacrifice. To you let the four quarters bow.

Griffith

Thine be the first oblations and the latter, entire, thy forceful shares of holy presents.
Let all this sacrifice be thine, O Agni, and let the world’s four regions how before thee.

Geldner

Dir sollen ausschlie├Яlich die Voropfer und die Nachopfer, die nahrhaften Teile des Opfers geh├╢ren. Dir, o Agni, soll dieses ganze Opfer geh├╢ren; vor dir sollen sich die vier Weltgegenden neigen!

Grassmann

Dein sei nun ganz der Vortrunk und der Nachtrunk, der nahrungsreiche Theil des Opfertrankes, Das ganze Opfer hier soll dein sein, Agni, und alle Lande sollen dir sich neigen.

Elizarenkova

рднрд╛рд╡рд╛рд░реНрдерднрд╛рд╖рд╛рдГ - рдордиреБрд╖реНрдп рдХреЗ рд╕рдорд╕реНрдд рдЦрд╛рди рдФрд░ рдкрд╛рди рдФрд░ рд╡рд┐рд╖рдпрднреЛрдЧ рд╕рдВрд╕рд╛рд░ рдореЗрдВ рдлрдБрд╕рдиреЗрд╡рд╛рд▓реЗ рди рд╣реЛрдВ, рдХрд┐рдиреНрддреБ рд╕рдЪреНрдЪреЗ рдХрд▓реНрдпрд╛рдг рдФрд░ рдореЛрдХреНрд╖ рдХреЗ рд╕рд╛рдзрди рдмрдиреЗрдВред рд╕рдорд╕реНрдд рджрд┐рд╢рд╛рдУрдВ рдХреА рдкреНрд░рдЬрд╛рдПрдБ рддреЗрд░реА рдкреНрд░рддрд┐рд╖реНрдард╛ рдХрд░реЗрдВ, рдРрд╕рд╛ рдЕрдкрдиреЗ рдХреЛ рдмрдирд╛ред рдПрд╡рдВ рд╡рд┐рджреНрдпреБрддреН рдХреЗ рдзрдирд╛рддреНрдордХ рдФрд░ рдЛрдгрд╛рддреНрдордХ рддрд╛рд░ рдЕрдкрдиреЗ-рдЕрдкрдиреЗ рд╕реНрдерд╛рди рдмрдиреНрдзрди рдореЗрдВ рдЕрд▓рдЧ-рдЕрд▓рдЧ рд╣реЛрдВ, рдЬреЛ рд╕рд╛рд░реА рдпрдиреНрддреНрд░ рдХреА рдХрд▓рд╛рдУрдВ рдХреЛ рд╕реНрд╡рд╛рдзреАрди рдХрд░рдХреЗ рдЪрд▓рд╛ рд╕рдХреЗрдВ реерепрее

рдмреНрд░рд╣реНрдордореБрдирд┐ - рдкрджрд╛рд░реНрдердГ

рдкрджрд╛рд░реНрдерд╛рдиреНрд╡рдпрднрд╛рд╖рд╛рдГ - (рдЕрдЧреНрдиреЗ) рд╣реЗ рдЕрдЩреНрдЧрд╛рдирд╛рдВ рдирд╛рдпрдХ ! рдЖрддреНрдордиреН (рддрд╡ рдкреНрд░рдпрд╛рдЬрд╛рдГ-рдЪ-рдЕрдиреБрдпрд╛рдЬрд╛рдГ-рдХреЗрд╡рд▓реЗ) рддрд╡ рдкреНрд░рдпрд╛рдЬрд╛рдГ рдкреНрд░рдХреГрд╖реНрдЯрднреЛрдХреНрддрд╡реНрдпрд╛ рдЕрдиреНрдирд╛рджрд┐рдкрджрд╛рд░реНрдерд╛рдГ, рддрдерд╛ рдЕрдиреБрдпрд╛рдЬрд╛рдГ рддрджрдиреБрд░реВрдкрдкреЗрдпрдкрджрд╛рд░реНрдерд╛рд╢реНрдЪ рдХреЗрд╡рд▓реЗ рдХреИрд╡рд▓реНрдпрд╕рд╛рдзрдиреЗ рднрд╡рдиреНрддреБ (рд╣рд╡рд┐рд╖рдГ-рднрд╛рдЧрд╛рдГ рдКрд░реНрдЬрд╕реНрд╡рдиреНрддрдГ рд╕рдиреНрддреБ) рдЧреНрд░рд╛рд╣реНрдпрд╕реНрдп рд╡рд┐рд╖рдпрд╕реНрдп рднрдЬрдиреАрдпрд╛ рдЕрдиреБрднрд╡рд╛рд╕реНрддреЗрдЬрд╕реНрд╡рд┐рдирдГ рд╕рдиреНрддреБ, рди рднреЛрдЧреЗ рдордЬреНрдЬрдпрдиреНрддреБ (рддрд╡-рдЕрдпрдВ рд╕рд░реНрд╡рдГ рдпрдЬреНрдЮрдГ-рдЕрд╕реНрддреБ) рдЕрдпрдВ рд╕рд░реНрд╡рдГ рд╢рд░реАрд░рдпрдЬреНрдЮрд╕реНрддрд╡ рдХрд▓реНрдпрд╛рдгрд╕рд╛рдзрдХреЛ рднрд╡рддреБ, рди рддрд╡ рдкреНрд░рддрд┐рдХреВрд▓рдВ рдЧрдЪреНрдЫреЗрддреН (рдЪрддрд╕реНрд░рдГ рдкреНрд░рджрд┐рд╢рдГ-рддреБрднреНрдпрдВ рдирдордиреНрддрд╛рдореН) рдЪрддрд╕реНрд░рдГ рдЪрддреБрд╖реНрдкреНрд░рдХрд╛рд░рд╛рдГ рдкреНрд░рдореБрдЦрджрд┐рдЧреНрд╡рд░реНрддрд┐рдиреНрдпрдГ рдкреНрд░рдЬрд╛рд╕реНрддреБрднреНрдпрдВ рдирдордиреНрддрд╛рдВ рд╕рддреНрдХреБрд░реНрд╡рдиреНрддреБред рддрдерд╛ (рдЕрдЧреНрдиреЗ) рд╣реЗ рд╡рд┐рджреНрдпреБрджреНрд░реВрдкрд╛рдЧреНрдиреЗ !
